The base price posted covers two guests or one queen bed. If another bed needs to be added for the second guest, it's the same as an additional guest fee of $10/night due to the extra work and laundry on our end. We also have a pack and play we can add for small guests. All additional guests over the first two are $10 extra per person a night (despite the age). This covers the additional bed(s), bedding, towels, wash cloths, and showers/bathing water that will be needed or take place.                         Located in Downtown Mesa, while we have plenty of great things to see and eat right here (Children's museums, Art Centers, food, lightrail), the best thing about Mesa is that we're just minutes away from 4 other amazing cities! We're 15 minutes from Downtown Tempe (Home of Arizona State University, food and bars). 15 Minutes from Downtown Gilbert, which is lined with tons of our favorite restaurants. We're 20 minutes from Downtown Scottsdale (Shopping galore, great hiking, bars, and food) and 20 minutes from Downtown Phoenix (Sports, food, music and museums). Arizona roads and freeways are super easy to navigate, so you can be anywhere you can imagine with ease! Ashley and I have done a lot of traveling internationally and domestically and while there are so many things we love about the places we've been, none of them have lived up to all the great food options we have here locally! We will provide you with a list of all our favorite local spots when you arrive.                        <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="900">
                        This unique home features the charm of a historic home while enjoying some modern updates. Not perfect but perfectly charming. It's spacious with over 2000sf. There's plenty of paved parking too. It's just around the corner from old town Mesa, very convenient to major freeways &amp; light-rail. This home has four bedrooms, each with comfy bedding &amp; mattresses and 2 full bathrooms with access in the hallways. When baseball fever hits the fields of Arizona this home will be a relaxing retreat.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="901">
                        This historic home was built in the 20's and is one of a kind. It has been updated throughout and has both modern amenities while keeping much of its historic charm. This unique home features four bedrooms, three of which have beds...a California king, one with a queen size bed, one with a full size bed &amp; one room has a hide-a-bed which is extra comfy with a memory foam topper. There's room for two to sleep on the extra large living room sofa too if needed. This home has a very large custom stone and tile shower in one bathroom and another bath with a European style tub/shower. Around the property you will see some of our projects. A couple of vintage Airstream travel trailers, an old stepside pickup truck... a shipping container. The home is on a busy street. Sometimes I notice the sound of traffic. The front bedroom we call the "Southwest Room" is the noisiest. We have earplugs for you if it's a bother. Have had great response with guests... please see reviews. We hope you choose to stay in our home and we look forward to hosting you!
                       </div>

                        The home is just minutes away from old town Mesa with unique shops and cultural facilities. There are many grocery stores in the area. The light rail is about 1 mile away which can take you across town including downtown Phoenix, the airport and many cultural &amp; sporting events.

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1030">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1031">
                        Queen bedroom and large window overlooking the backyard fig tree on the upper floor of a blue Victorian style house at the end of a quiet cul-de-sac in a charming neighborhood of architecturally unique homes located between the Cubs stadium and Oakland A's stadium and historic downtown Mesa but also not far from the ASU campus, Downtown Tempe, and Old Town Scottsdale. Adjacent full bathroom with tub. Adjacent bedroom has 4 bunks suitable for adults or kids. Bunks can be added to the reservation.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1032">
                        Suite sleeps up to 6 in two rooms: This is a large bedroom with a queen size bed that sleeps one or two, dresser with a full private bath (including tub) next door. The adjacent room with adjoining access has four bunk beds suitable for adults or children. NOTE: Our base price is for up to two people both in the queen bed together and using only the queen bedroom space. We do not automatically prepare the bunks or the bunk room for guest use unless at least one bunk is being rented. Please let us know if you'd like to add bunks. Thank you!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1033">
                        Our home is located between the Cubs and Oakland A's stadiums (1.5 miles to each), Riverview Shopping and Park, downtown Mesa, the Mesa Convention Center, and the Mesa Arts Center, Tempe Market Place, ASU and downtown Tempe, Old Town Scottsdale, freeways 202, 101, and the 60 and various places to board Valley Metro, the one-ticket public transportation including the light rail and bus system. There is also a free shuttle downtown bus that runs less frequently with a stop that is even closer to us than the Valley Metro bus stop.

                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1349">
                        Soak up the Arizona Sunshine at this beautiful condo in Mesa GPA. Great location, close to Cubs training camp, Old Town Scottsdale, shopping, dining, golfing and more, or just enjoy the warm weather at one of the 2 complex pools and hot tubs.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1350">
                        One of a kind floor plan in a gorgeous condo complex features 1500 sq ft of open concept living. Full kitchen, dining and living space, 2 bedrooms plus loft and two full baths. Loft has a futon and can be used as a second living room, and/or sleeping space for up to 2 people. Master suite has brand new King Size bed, attached bath with a pool side view. Condo comes equipped with washer/dryer and all major appliances. Also enjoy a single car attached garage.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1351">
                        Conveniently located close to other major communities; Scottsdale, Tempe and Chandler. 10 minute drive to Airport with quick access to nearby freeways. Chicago Cubs Spring Training is nearby as are the two river walk outdoor shopping malls within 5 minutes drive. We are also a short drive away from some great lakes. Make a day trip out to Canyon Lake and check out Tortilla flats or keep going to Roosevelt and check out the dam. Be prepared for less than stellar road conditions as you follow We are around the corner from the Mesa Amphitheater, who plays host to many great outdoor concerts. 
                       </div>

                        <li data-reactid="1377"><p data-reactid="1378">I had a little bit of difficulty getting in the front door but Lindsay was quick to respond and assist me in figuring out the key pad. If you prefer a soft - medium mattress you may not find the beds all that comfortable. They are pretty stiff. I actually ended up taking the futon off of the small den upstairs and putting it on top of the bed which worked out really well. If you like a firm mattress, you'll be just fine. I also had a little difficulty with the thermostat because its a NEST (which is great but I should have checked it out before going to sleep). The automatic schedule on the thermostat was set at midnight to go to over 75 degrees so I woke up extremely hot and sweating and had to figure out how to work it in the middle of the night. If I had paid more attention I would have figured that out before bed. Additionally, I ended up moving to the upstairs bedroom because there is no curtain on the top of the window in the master and the sun rises very early and the bedroom is on the east side of the house. At night the lights from the pool create a good bit of light pollution. If light bothers you while you sleep, bring night blinders. Besides a few hiccups, the condo was convenient, clean, and very quiet. Lindsay was easy to work with and available whenever needed. The small pool was closed when I was there, but the larger one was open and it was really beautiful. All in all, I think this is a good place to stay in Mesa for the price.</p><span data-reactid="1379">Amy</span><span data-reactid="1380">2016-04-14T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                        <li data-reactid="2149"><p data-reactid="2150">We rented this home to have a space for my family to stay during my wedding. The open great room/dining room/kitchen met our needs for gathering/spending family time together, and it was a nice space and a good layout. This home would be better suited for a family with children vs. all adults. The sleeping accommodations ideally fit about 6 adults - anything more than that involves cots, pull-outs, or floor mattresses which may be fine for children, but are not ideal for older adults. There is also limited parking, so having multiple adults coming from various parts of the country can be a challenge if there are more than 3 cars involved. In comparison to other spaces we’ve rented in the past, this space would not score as well regarding making us feel comfortable. When it is approaching 100 degrees out and there are 11 people in the space, it can get quite warm and uncomfortable. We paid a market premium price because it was spring training week, but I would have preferred that the cost to cool the space to a comfortable level be built into the cost of the rental as well. It was a lot of money to pay to not have the temperature comfortable for my family. It was the first time we rented a family’s primary residence (vs. a rental or guest property/space) and we tried to be very respectful of their space and their things. We treated the home like we would want someone to treat ours and I realize not everyone does that, which I imagine is the reason there are so many rules and restrictions posted. Many of the rules were made clear when we booked the initial rental and we have no issue with respecting the wishes of the homeowner, but we weren’t prepared for it to feel so unwelcoming or be so lacking in basic provisions such as enough towels and pillows. If there was more balance between an emphasis on the rules and an equal emphasis on making the guests feel welcome, it would be a better experience. Little touches that some B&amp;Bs utilize (such as baskets of toiletries, having ample towels, pillow options, a nice welcome note that tells you where to find linens and which dishes to use, etc.) would be a nice way to make guests feel more welcome.
